They literally couldn't do anything with the F13 lawsuit, they couldn't even add a new tree or a rock to a map, a developer literally said this. Its understandable why they eventually gave up, they were just waiting around doing nothing while two guys argued over money and a settlement.  As for TCM I never bought it (so far), but them abandoning support for it so soon, I agree it is bad. However, Illfonic had nothing to do with TCM so I see more hope for this. Carpenter is also credited as an executive producer which is a major bonus.  Also, for those complaining that the singleplayer experience will either just be offline bots, something like the F13 challenges, or the virtual cabin, literally do your research morons. The Halloween Game website literally says it in black and white:  "IllFonic dives into why making a singleplayer narrative in Halloween was a must. The narrative for singleplayer in Halloween takes on a new shape. Playing as Michael Myers, walk through memorable locations from the 1978 classic such as the Myers House or bask in the recreated atmosphere of Haddonfield".  Lets just see how it plays out and actually give it a chance before prematurely calling it a failure. I'm a huge Halloween fan, I see Halloween and I'm there for it Day 1. If its anywhere near as fun as F13 was (which was waaaaay more fun than Dead By Daylight regardless of the bugs/glitches) this will be awesome.  If it happens a 2nd time (like with TCM) then yeah there's a pattern forming. Call me a sucker or whatever, but its Halloween, as a fan of the series I can't not be there for this. Especially since it has a singleplayer mode.
